***brutus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brutus.html>brutus</a> (8435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>An</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Oscan language">Oscan</a></span> loanword, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*g ∑r√©h‚ÇÇus</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a> (3833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1802, colloquial <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">butty</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:companion.html>companion</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:older.html>older</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dialect.html>dialect</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> workmate, associated <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:coal.html>coal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mining.html>mining</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>Itself</a> believed derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 1530 <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:booty.html>booty</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fellow.html>fellow</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partner.html>partner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> whom <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> shares <a href = vnd.unilang:booty.html>booty</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loot.html>loot</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Alternatively, <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> alteration <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:brother.html>brother</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***bugel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bugel.html>bugel</a> (40985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <small>[<a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>Term</a>?]</small>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">b≈´culus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugel.html>bugel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugels.html>bugels</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugel.html>bugeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buik.html>buik</a> (2280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buuc</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">b≈´c</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*b≈´kaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buik.html>buik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buiken.html>buiken</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buikje.html>buikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
